3 of 9
   eta_e_2 = A_0 + A_1*log(vflow_out_wf_e_2) + A_2*VR_e_single_2
   
   
   %Poweroutput is subdivided for first stage in series for the volume flow m^3/J with
   %volume flow fractions
   fraction_1 = vflow_out_wf_e_1 / (vflow_out_wf_e_1 + vflow_out_wf_e_2)
   P_2_stage_1 = ((P_e/eta_g)/(1*10^6)) * fraction_1
   
   VC_total_1 = vflow_out_wf_e_1/ P_2_stage_1 %total volume flow m^3/J
   n_e_stages_VC_e_1 = ceil(VC_total_1 / vflow_out_e_single_VC)    
   
   C_expander_single_1 =3143.7+217423*vflow_out_wf_e_1;
   C_expander_1 =C_expander_single_1*n_e_stages_VC_e_1;
   
   %Poweroutput is subdivided for second stage in series for the volume flow m^3/J with
   %volume flow fractions
   
   fraction_2 = vflow_out_wf_e_2 / (vflow_out_wf_e_1 + vflow_out_wf_e_2)
   P_2_stage_2 = ((P_e/eta_g)/(1*10^6)) * fraction_2
   
   VC_total_2 = vflow_out_wf_e_2/ P_2_stage_2 %total volume flow m^3/J
   n_e_stages_VC_e_2 = ceil(VC_total_2 / vflow_out_e_single_VC)
   
   C_expander_single_2 =3143.7+217423*vflow_out_wf_e_2;
   C_expander_2 =C_expander_single_2*n_e_stages_VC_e_2;
   
   %efficiencies and number of stages are calculated
   eta_e = eta_e_1 * eta_e_2 
   VC_total = VC_total_1 + VC_total_2
   n_e_stages = n_e_stages_VC_e_1 + n_e_stages_VC_e_2
   
   C_expander = C_expander_1 + C_expander_2
   
   elseif n_e_stages_VR_limit==3
   
       
   %first stage in series    
   VR_e_single_1 = 5    
   rho_out_wf_e_1 = rho_in_wf_e / VR_e_single_1
   vflow_out_wf_e_1 = mflow_wf / rho_out_wf_e_1
   eta_e_1 = A_0 + A_1*log(vflow_out_wf_e_1) + A_2*VR_e_single_1
   
   %second stage in series
   
   VR_e_single_2 = 5
   rho_in_wf_e_2 = rho_out_wf_e_1
   rho_out_wf_e_2 = rho_in_wf_e_2 / VR_e_single_2
   vflow_out_wf_e_2 = mflow_wf / rho_out_wf_e_2
   eta_e_2 = A_0 + A_1*log(vflow_out_wf_e_2) + A_2*VR_e_single_2
   
   %third stage in series

   rho_in_wf_e_3 = rho_out_wf_e_2
   rho_out_wf_e_3 = rho_in_wf_e_3 / VR_e_single
   vflow_out_wf_e_3 = mflow_wf / rho_out_wf_e_3
   eta_e_3 = A_0 + A_1*log(vflow_out_wf_e_3) + A_2*VR_e_single_3
 
   
   %Poweroutput is subdivided for first stage in series for the volume flow m^3/J with

   fraction_1 = vflow_out_wf_e_1 / (vflow_out_wf_e_1 + vflow_out_wf_e_2 + 
vflow_out_wf_e_3)
   P_2_stage_1 = ((P_e/eta_g)/(1*10^6)) * fraction_1

   n_e_stages_VC_e_1 = ceil(VC_total_1 / vflow_out_e_single_VC)

vflow_out_wf_e_3)
   P_2_stage_2 = ((P_e/eta_g)/(1*10^6)) * fraction_2
   
   VC_total_2 = vflow_out_wf_e_2/ P_2_stage_2 %total volume flow m^3/J
   n_e_stages_VC_e_2 = ceil(VC_total_2 / vflow_out_e_single_VC)

   C_expander_2 =C_expander_single_2*n_e_stages_VC_e_2;

   VC_total_3 = vflow_out_wf_e_3/ P_2_stage_3 %total volume flow m^3/J
   n_e_stages_VC_e_3 = ceil(VC_total_3 / vflow_out_e_single_VC)
   
   C_expander_single_3 =3143.7+217423*vflow_out_wf_e_3;
   C_expander_3 =C_expander_single_3*n_e_stages_VC_e_3;

   VC_total = VC_total_1 + VC_total_2 + VC_total_3

   eta_e = eta_e_1 * eta_e_2 * eta_e_3 * eta_e_4 * eta_e_5
   
   VC_total = VC_total_1 + VC_total_2 + VC_total_3 + VC_total_4 + VC_total_5
   n_e_stages = n_e_stages_VC_e_1 + n_e_stages_VC_e_2 + n_e_stages_VC_e_3 + 
n_e_stages_VC_e_4 + n_e_stages_VC_e_5
   
   C_expander = C_expander_1 + C_expander_2 + C_expander_3 + C_expander_4 + C_expander_5
   
 
   end
end

    C_Motor_0 = C_Motor_0_min*(P_f_cs/eta_f_cs/P_min)^(1-0.67);
elseif P_f_cs/eta_f_cs > P_max
    display('Motor power out of bounds')
    C_Motor_0_max = 603.1/397*10^(K1 + K2*log10(P_max/1000) + K3*(log10(P_max/1000))^2);
    C_Motor_0 = C_Motor_0_max*(P_f_cs/eta_f_cs/P_max)^(1-0.1);
end
ID_BM = 13;
F_BM = F_bm(ID_BM);
C_motor_pump_cs = C_Motor_0*(F_BM);
 
P_pi = P_f_cs/eta_f_cs/eta_pi_cs;
K1 = 2.9573;
K2 = 0.2783;
K3 = 0.1452;
C_inverter_pump_cs = 603.1/394.1*10^(K1 + K2*log10(P_pi/1000) + K3*(log10(P_pi/1000)));
 
==PAGE:194==
29-06-21 09:22
C:\MATLAB\computeCosts.m
10 of 10
% Total purchase costs in USD
C_BM = C_eva + C_k + C_p + C_motor_pump + C_inverter_pump + C_p_hs + C_motor_pump_hs + 
C_inverter_pump_hs + C_p_cs + C_motor_pump_cs + C_inverter_pump_cs + C_turbine + 
C_generator + C_rec;
C_p_tot = C_p + C_motor_pump + C_inverter_pump;
C_p_hs_tot = C_p_hs + C_motor_pump_hs + C_inverter_pump_hs;
C_p_cs_tot = C_p_cs + C_motor_pump_cs + C_inverter_pump_cs;
C_t_tot = C_turbine + C_generator;
costs = [C_eva; C_k; C_p_tot; C_t_tot; C_rec; C_p_hs_tot; C_p_cs_tot];
C_fixed = C_BM;
